Important evidence includes whether the equipment is energized, whether the guard is missing or removed, whether the exposed part is reachable during normal work, and whether lockout/tagout or blocking is required before correction. Recommended controls include restricting access, stopping exposure, repairing or installing guarding, verifying energy isolation where maintenance is involved, and documenting closure with photo evidence.',
